    <h1 class="heading">
     Description
    </h1>
    <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description">
     <div class="id-app-orig-desc">
      The Original Panic Popping game!
      <p>
       Panic Pop started from my own fears. It originally was meant to help those who were suffering from panic disorder, a disease that causes violent and often unexpected panic attacks that are reinforced by negative thoughts (like "I'm definitely going to have a heart attack" or "That guy is following me and going to murder my brain"). Since I am a suffer of this disorder, I wanted to do something about these awful experiences. So I made Panic Pop. The entire point of this game is to suck you in. It's meant to be something that requires your entire focus. It should not let you set it down.
      </p>
      <p>
       The thought was that if the player could set the game down, they could go back to panicking. So I hope, with all my heart, whether you are a panic attack sufferer or just a regular bloke, that you will be immersed and consumed by my game. Good luck!
      </p>
      <p>
       Don't let the bubbles shrink.
      </p>
     </div>
     <div class="show-more-end">
     </div>
    </div>

           <br/>

               MAIN FEATURES of Jelly Dash Extreme (Sugar Line Rush)    
           <br/>
            3 game modes: Action, Endless, and Challenge. Gameplay is in Time Mode. Try to get your best score before time over!
           <br/>
            Maximize your points in 120-second Action mode. You can get extra time in special jelly.
           <br/>
            Try to pass as many levels as you can in Endless &amp; Challenge mode. Each level you have a target score and 70 seconds to play.

           <br/>

           <br/>
           Thunder Horizontal to clear row of sugar jelly
           <br/>
           Extra Time (add 5 seconds)
           <br/>
           Color Pop to blast all sugar jelly have save color
           <br/>
           Double Score you get in 8 seconds
           <br/>

           <br/>

           <br/>
            Lovely background music &amp; interaction sound

           <br/>
            Jelly Link: connect 3 or more same jellies to explode them. The more sweet Jelly you link, the more score you have, but be quickly before time over!
           <br/>
            Special extra score: move gift box to the bottom of the puzzle to get more scores
           <br/>
            Power-ups: when boosters appear on Jelly, try to connect to get them. The booster will activate directly on your fingertips! The boosters include bomb, thunder, extra time, super color pop, double score
           <br/>
            Action mode: try to get your best score in nearly 2 minutes &amp; then compare with other players on Facebook or global Leader Board.
           <br/>
